np.array([float(val) for val in line[1:]])\n        vk = vk @ rtv\n        if i == 0:\n            kpath.append(0.0)\n        else:\n            kpath.append(kpath[i-1] + np.sqrt(np.dot(vk - oldvk, vk - oldvk)))\n        oldvk = vk[:]\n        eigs.append(np.array([(float(val)-ChemP)*27.2113845 for val in file.readline().split()]))\n\nbands = []\nfor i in range(int(maxneig)):\n    band = []\n
